# Quarkus GraphQL schema creator StackOverflow Reproducer

A reproducer for GraphQL schema creator StackOverflow exception.

Used in issue _TBA_.

## Steps to reproduce

Just run the application to reproduce the issue.

```
$ mvn quarkus:dev
```
